# SlopScale Roadmap

> Read this at the start of every session. Update it before closing.
> Current date: 2026-06-12.

## üî≠ Host-release overlap sweep (STANDING RITUAL ‚Äî run on every new Slopsmith release)

SlopScale keeps building things the host later ships (v0.2.9 shipped a Tuner, Drums, Minigames XP, NAM Rig Builder, settings export, wake-lock ‚Äî we'd hand-built our own of all six). The per-feature HOST CHECK fires once at design time and can't catch a clean build *becoming* a double-build when the host later ships parity. So: **when a new Slopsmith Desktop/host release lands, do a ~15-min overlap sweep** (this is the standing counterpart to the per-feature HOST CHECK in CLAUDE.md rule 4):
1. Read the host release notes ‚Üí list new capabilities.
2. Cross-check each against the **watchlist** below (our shell features the host might ship). For every overlap, make ONE call: **migrate-to-borrow** (host's is now good enough ‚Äî retire ours) ¬∑ **keep-ours-with-a-written-reason** (e.g. our tuner is target-aware + contained-playback-scoped) ¬∑ **defer**.
3. Re-verify our borrows still work on the new build: `SLOPSMITH_SOURCE=bundled npm test` (tests our `main` against the actual user runtime) + an eyeball launch.

**Watchlist ‚Äî shell capabilities we OWN that the host might ship (flip to borrow when host parity arrives):**
tuner (ours = target-aware) ¬∑ drums (ours = synth/WAF, no host bank to borrow live) ¬∑ XP/progress (ours = competency-typed; host = flat sqrt-score ‚Üí DON'T feed; host-subscribes-to-our-emit is the on-mission path) ¬∑ mixer (ours = per-instrument buses; host mix-plane is plugin-output-level + player-gated) ¬∑ wake-lock ¬∑ settings export ¬∑ NAM tone (host borrow now GREEN ‚Äî runtime-only, never vendor) ¬∑ scoring/detector (host territory ‚Äî we never build DSP) ¬∑ asset-serving (host generic asset route exists; low-value migrate).
> The slopsmith-host-expert + devops agents carry the live version of this watchlist in their memory. Full v0.2.9 audit: project memory `project_host_release_v029_audit`.

## Session log (most recent first)

### ‚è∏Ô∏è STOPPED HERE (2026-06-13 session #32) ‚Äî metal Lead-Over-the-Band + B1 ARRANGEMENT_RECIPES (9 genres) + audio fixes + REAL CAB IRs + the AMP/CAB "RIG" view ‚Üí **beta `v0.7.24-beta.6`**. dev `0.7.24-dev`; `main` still v0.7.23 (beta-only).
> **B1 GENRE-RECIPE BATCH ‚Äî 9 genres AUTHORED (in beta.6), each instrument IDIOMATIC per role (Christian's mandate: "not boring whole-note chords + four-on-the-floor for everything").** Wave 1: **blues** (boogie_stab/bass_ostinato/shuffle_blues), **jazz** (charleston/walking/jazz_swing), **rock** (rock_chug/root_pump/straight_8th_rock + sparse vamp_half/two_feel), **gospel** (charleston/walking/gospel_pocket). Batch 2 (funk-idiom + country-idiom + pop-idiom + bass-pedagogy): **funk** (NEW `funk_chank_16` comp + NEW `funk_pocket_16` bass [bass-ped corrected] + `funk_16th` drums ‚Äî NEVER a straight-8th/four-floor kit), **country** (NEW `country_chuck` comp + `two_feel` bass + `train_beat` ‚Äî bass-ped split: BASS booms via two_feel, GUITAR chucks, not both), **pop** (`pop_push`/`root_pump`/`straight_8th_rock` ‚Äî DEFAULT pop is 8th-strum NOT four-on-the-floor; + a dormant `pop:dance:groove` four-floor key). Added `funk`/`pop`/`country` `audioProfile`s (clav/epiano/clean ‚Äî were null/shared) so the comp plays an idiomatic VOICE. **VERIFIED: the recipe fires only where a chord timeline runs (lead/scale + Jam) ‚Äî riff drills emit no comp/bass (no clash).** Non-regressive; `smoke-backing-engine` 6f covers all 9 + a "pop ‚âÝ four-on-the-floor" mandate assert. **NEXT (B1 remaining): bluegrass + city-pop recipes; the flagged cell GAPS ‚Äî `gospel_shout` (praise-break drum), `gospel_12_8` (triplet ballad comp), `octave_jump_bass` (dance-pop bounce), rock `punk_down8` + quiet‚Üíloud auto-arc; the `metal_double_kick` metal-recipe upgrade.** Memory [[project_arrangement_recipes_b1]].
> **AMP/CAB "RIG" VIEW (3-agent design pass + v1 BUILT, in beta.4):** the Mixer's `[Console | Rig]` second tab ‚Äî per-amp (Clean/Overdrive/Metal) user **cab-IR upload** (file picker ‚Üí IndexedDB) + **Output** trim, for the BACKING band. `ensureCabIr` resolves `user:<amp>` from IndexedDB before the `/ir/` fetch (same hot-swap/fallback); `buildAmpChain(ctx,p,ampId)` applies the per-amp cab+output override; persist bytes‚ÜíIndexedDB `slopscale-rig`, meta‚ÜílocalStorage `slopscale.rig`. Player's LIVE amp stays the Input "YOU"‚Üí"Tone‚Ä¶" handoff to nam_tone (band tone ‚âÝ live tone). probe-rig 10/10 + 18/18 + core-purity green. **HOST CHECK (verified): NAM engine/A2/player-presets = BORROW (nam_tone worklet is cross-plugin + A2 loads free; `/presets`+`/file/model|ir` readable); GUI = BUILD ours; live-amp = defer to nam_tone.** Full design + decisions: `docs/amp-cab-roundtable.md`, memory [[project_amp_cab_rig_and_nam_a2]].
> **AMP-TONE CUSTOMIZATION = a STAGED future track (power-user requests land here; do NOT rabbit-hole).** The process: ship defaults (Stage 0 DONE ‚Äî presets + V30 IR + Rig cab-upload/output) ‚Üí revisit one safe stage at a time, each gated on real demand: **v1.1** Drive/EQ macros (params already in AMP_PRESETS) ‚Üí **"use my NAM tone"** (read the player's nam_tone presets straight into a backing amp; A2 free ‚Äî the compelling NAM tier) ‚Üí generic NAM/A2 model load (gated; A2-Lite, one lazy worklet) ‚Üí **source CC0 clean/crunch cabs to ship** (the REAL backing-tone win ‚Äî clean/OD are procedural in the public build) ‚Üí built-in cab library. Staged in `docs/amp-cab-roundtable.md`.
> **REAL CAB IRs (per-preset, COMMITTED + in beta.3):** the amp chain's single PROCEDURAL cab ‚Üí a per-preset real cab IR with the procedural as fallback. `AMP_PRESETS[*].ir` + `ensureCabIr` (lazy `/ir/<name>.wav` fetch‚Üídecode‚Üíhot-swap the convolver buffer; 404/absent ‚Üí procedural stays). **Metal = Celestion V30 4√ó12** (`v30_4x12.wav`, Deer Ink Studios via [AIDA-X](https://github.com/AidaDSP/AIDA-X), **GPL-3** ‚Üí AGPL-compatible) ‚Äî **SHIPS** (gitignore `static/irs/*` + `!v30_4x12.wav` + `!README.md`). **Clean = GGD Zilla "Boutique Clean"**, **Overdrive = Marshall JMP2203** ‚Äî Christian's lib, COMMERCIAL ‚Üí **local-only** (gitignored; the public/remote build falls back to procedural for these two, his builds get all three). Role-named files = hot-swappable. Provenance: `static/irs/README.md`. probe-cab-ir 8/8 + 18/18 smoke. **Open-source hunt result (the genuine wall): redistributable IRs of those exact amps barely exist ‚Äî only V30 was findable CC0/GPL; a CC0 clean-Fender / Greenback is still open (Soundwoofer is the candidate but its per-file license is unconfirmed).** NEXT: if a CC0 clean/Marshall turns up, drop it at `cab_clean.wav`/`cab_drive.wav` + un-gitignore to ship. **Desktop beta drop gets the local cabs copied in manually (cut-beta only copies tracked files).**

All by-ear FIRST-PASS ‚Äî **awaiting Christian's re-judge on beta.2.** Other open by-ear gates (carried): the amp presets' overall tone, FluidR3 timbre.
> **B1 ARRANGEMENT_RECIPES (band-intel Track B ‚Äî COMMITTED, 18/18 green):** the recipe layer so a STYLE declares its band instead of pathways hand-wiring it. `ARRANGEMENT_RECIPES` (pure data, keyed `style:feel:densityTier`, pointers onto COMP_GROOVES/BASS_FIGURES/DRUM_GROOVES) + `resolveArrangement(cfg)` (mirrors `resolveAudioProfile`) wired as the FINAL default in `compCellForConfig`/`bassFigureForConfig`/`resolveGroove` ‚Äî **additive/non-regressive** (authored `cfg.backing*` + boogie/swing routes always win; un-recipe'd styles return empty picks ‚Üí old logic). Pilots: **metal + djent only** (match today's picks; the metal-lead pathways still hand-wire, so byte-identical). Density tiers sparse/groove/full = the future section-FSM mask. `validateArrangementRecipes` guard + `smoke-backing-engine` phase 6f. core-purity still green (resolveArrangement is pure). **NEXT for B1: the genre-recipe AUTHORING BATCH** (blues/jazz/funk/rock/‚Ä¶ recipes, each its idiom agent's call + the `metal_double_kick` drum upgrade for metal ‚Äî vetted, NOT silent); then migrate hand-wired pathways to recipe-driven; B2 = mix deltas/latch/swaps. > **BUILD (done, session #32) ‚Äî the metal LEAD-over-backing pack** (panel: metal-idiom owns ¬∑ learning-design chairs ¬∑ harmony ¬∑ guitar-pedagogy; all four memos logged). The application layer the Metal pack was missing (it was all riff-drills, no "solo over the band") AND the live trigger that makes the distorted-comp realism sound. **Shipped:** (1) 3 `COMP_GROOVES` cells ‚Äî `metal_chug_8` (8th power-5th chug, the rung-1 default), `metal_pedal_16` (djent 16th pedal), `metal_gallop` ‚Äî all on `root5` (3rd-less power 5ths = the only clean-under-gain voicing; `rock_chug`'s rings are anti-metal); (2) `root5` anchor lowered 48‚Üí40 so the comp sits UNDER the lead (harmony's ‚â§midi-52 ruling; root5 was unused by any shipped cell, so safe); (3) 2 new guitar PATHWAYS ‚Äî **`metal_lead_changes`** (E nat-minor over `metal_i_bVI_bVII`, `metal_chug_8`+`root_pump` bass, **metal** profile, standard tuning, fret-11‚Äì15 box, ~100) and **`metal_lead_phrygian`** (E phrygian over a static `phrygian_vamp`, `metal_pedal_16`, **djent** profile, ~105 ‚Äî the ‚ô≠2 "drop"); LEAD stays clean DI in STANDARD tuning, decoupled from the heavy backing (guitar-pedagogy: the "lead must use the low open string" rule is for one-player-covers-both, N/A here); (4) wired into `style_metal` band + 3 `SKILL_TREE_EDGES` (gallop‚Üíchanges‚Üíphrygian‚Üí`djent_lock_the_cell` jam cap) + 2 `<option>`s; (5) a Workout SEGMENT_TEMPLATE `g_metal_lead` (application role); (6) a durable `smoke-backing-engine` phase 6e (7 asserts ‚Äî comp emits `metal_chug_8` on low root5 + `root_pump` bass + metal-amp resolves + synth pad kept). **Verify:** `probe-distorted-comp.mjs` 10/10 now points at the SHIPPED `metal_lead_changes` (no overrides ‚Äî 64 lead notes, 64 comp hits double-tracked 184√ó, 64 bass events, Metal bus wired); **full `npm test` 18/18** (backing-engine 94‚Üí101, variation 66‚Üí67). **HOST CHECK: N/A** (content over existing verified engines).
> **VERIFY (session #32, pre-build):** the distorted-comp plumbing was confirmed correct before the build ‚Äî the two prior probe "FAILs" were PROBE BUGS (wrong rung `metalcore_chug` emits no comp + wrong artifact: `makeBundle` assembles `backingEvents`, not `generateExercise().chart`). That verification is what surfaced the KEY FINDING below.
> **KEY FINDING ‚Äî the headline realism was CORRECT but DORMANT (now LIT by the build above).** Nothing shipped emits distorted comp: metal/djent pathways are RIFF DRILLS (`rhythm_pulse`/`pedal_riff`, anchor-based, `backingStyle:'pad'` ‚Üí synth-pad backing, `compCellForConfig`‚Üínull), and `strum_comp` suppresses backing comp. The ONLY trigger is a LEAD/scale activity over a metal PROGRESSION with a comp groove (had to force it: `blues_shuffle` + override profile‚Üídjent + `backingComp`‚Üí`rock_chug`). Same dormancy for guitar `n.mt`‚Üí`sg_mutestr` (mt ghosts only come from the slap-BASS builder, and bass forces the non-DI voice) and the `chuck` samples (no `COMP_GROOVES` cell uses `a:'chuck'`). LIVE-now pieces of the changeset: shiny DI guide (shipped), distorted Keys staying synth (`pad` slot), accent-aware strum stagger.
> **DECISION (Christian, session #32): BUILD A LIVE TRIGGER FIRST ‚Äî don't land dormant code.** Add a 'metal/djent LEAD over a chugging rhythm-section backing' context (the player solos while the band chugs a double-tracked DI-through-Metal rhythm guitar) so the realism actually sounds, vet with the panel, commit it all as one live feature. **HOST CHECK: N/A** (content over existing verified engines ‚Äî backing comp + amp + double-track already built; no new shell capability). **Panel** (metal-idiom owns ¬∑ learning-design chairs ¬∑ harmony ¬∑ guitar-pedagogy) ran, synthesized, BUILT ‚Äî see the BUILD bullet at the top. **DONE:** committed `67a22f4` + pushed dev + beta `v0.7.24-beta.1` (branch + Desktop). **NEXT:** Christian dogfoods the beta (clean lead over the double-tracked metal comp + the open amp-preset gates); when happy ‚Üí promote dev‚Üímain + version-bump (`plugin.json` + `SLOPSCALE_VERSION` ‚Üí `0.7.24`) + tag + GitHub release.

> **SESSION #29 DETAIL:**

On a high-gain/compressed/sustained **DI** the level envelope is flat ‚Üí a re-pick is only a few dB over the ringing baseline ‚Üí no onset fires ‚Üí **every note after the first was rejected**. > - **Step 0 ‚Äî voice rename to the host `lib/drums.py` PIECES vocabulary** (snake_case): `hatClosed‚Üíhh_closed`(42) `hatOpen‚Üíhh_open`(46) `hatPedal‚Üíhh_pedal`(44) `crash‚Üícrash_l`(49) `tomHi/Mid/Lo‚Üítom_hi/mid/low`; ADDED `snare_xstick`(37) `tom_floor`(41) `ride_bell`(53) `crash_r`(57) `china`(52) `splash`(55) `bell`(80). A SlopScale drum event now maps 1:1 onto the host's 18-piece kit. Renamed across `ACOUSTIC_PIECES`/`DRUM_CORE_PIECES`/`DRUM_GROOVES`/`chokeOpenHats`/`buildGenericDrumGroove`/`DRUM_NATURAL_DUR`/`scheduleDrumHit`/`scheduleSynthDrumHit`.
> - **Step 1 ‚Äî schema:** per-lane `{pat,vel,div}` (quiet kit + a 16th double-kick under an 8th hat); tokens `x`=feathered/whisper ¬∑ `o`=open-hat (‚Üíhh_open) ¬∑ `f`=flam (grace+main); `cellBars` (multi-bar clave); `preSwung` swing-lock; **`FILLS` registry** + `fillFamily`/`fillEveryBars` (default 8) ‚Äî a fill swaps the phrase's last bar, mutes the time-keeping hats, drops a `crash_l` on the next downbeat; **`comp[]`** seed-rotated jazz snare overlay; **`DRUM_PIECE_GAIN`** per-piece relative gain (ride 0.5 / foot 0.3 / snare 1.0 ‚Äî applied in BOTH drum engines, tames the hot GM ride).
> - **Step 2 ‚Äî 8 grooves:** `jazz_swing` (spang-a-lang ride + hi-hat foot 2&4 + feathered kick + comp[], NO backbeat snare) ¬∑ `reggae_one_drop` ¬∑ `funk_16th` ¬∑ `metal_double_kick` (per-lane div:4 double-bass) ¬∑ `train_beat` ¬∑ `gospel_pocket` ¬∑ `bossa` (2-bar clave) ¬∑ `second_line` (2-bar). Kept the original 4 (lanes renamed).
> - **Step 3 ‚Äî routing:** `resolveGroove` is style-keyed (`GROOVE_FOR_PROFILE` jazz‚Üíjazz_swing) and reads the profile from BOTH `cfg.audioProfile` and `cfg.audio.profile` (`cfgAudioProfile`). **Deliberately does NOT route a bare `swing:'swing'`‚Üíjazz** (jazz-idiom). Added `audioProfile:'jazz'` to the two swung jazz pathways that lacked it (`vl_connect`, `ii_V_I_workout`). Drumless via opt-in `cfg.drums:'none'` (NOT by token ‚Äî `bluegrass` is shared by country, which has a drummer).
> - **Step 4 ‚Äî seeded humanization** (`humanizeDrums`, salt `^0x4452554d` so it never correlates with the bass roll): ¬±3‚Äì8 ms micro-timing + velocity jitter, baked before swing, the loop's "one" protected (no flam vs the wrap), electronic kits √ó0.2 (machines are tight). **Determinism is a hard rule** (same cfg ‚áí byte-identical events).
> - **Step 5 ‚Äî synth voices** for the new lanes (`ride` warm tip / `ride_bell`+`bell` / `snare_xstick` woody / `hh_pedal` dark foot / `tom_floor` / `crash_r`/`splash`/`china`). **`SAMPLED_DRUM_NOTES` gate**: the 7 new pieces have no committed FluidR3 one-shot ‚Üí they take the synth voice instead of a per-hit 404 (loadWafPreset retries on 'failed'). The core kit (kick/snare/hats/toms/ride/crash_l/hh_pedal) still plays SAMPLED.
> - **Step 6 (partial) ‚Äî mix:** per-piece gain table (above) ¬∑ drums on the shared reverb send (~0.07) + a ‚àí0.1 pan (refactored the shared reverb into `ensureSharedReverb` so either bus can create it) ¬∑ crash 7 ms soft-attack ramp. **Deferred (by-ear refinements the plan flagged): kit-class-aware jazz high-shelf (6.5‚Äì7 kHz) switching** (needs per-config bus reconfig) **+ crash cross-bus coupling-trim.**

> - **‚≠ê Timing-judging Slice 2 BUILT (2026-06-06 session #13 ‚Äî the fast-idiom honesty layer; full build record in the roundtable doc).** **Probes ran FIRST** (`probe-verifier-envelope.mjs`, 9 scenarios + a wrong-pitch negative control): verifier **min-ring ‚âà 50ms** (200 BPM 16ths honestly judgeable in verifier mode) ¬∑ **palm-mute SURVIVES the comb** (100% ‚Äî no PM exemption needed) ¬∑ the verifier has **NO 70Hz floor** (E1+B0 100% ‚Äî the sub-floor exemption dissolves in verifier mode; YIN keeps it). **Shipped:** per-ear `tooFast` floor (YIN 85ms / verifier 50ms) on an **effective ring** (written-staccato `sus<0.7¬∑IOI` rings sus ‚Äî the bass anti-pedagogy headline fixed by DISCLOSURE; legato-ish runs ring IOI ‚Äî chart sus can't self-exempt the 160-BPM acceptance; last note rings free) ‚Üí exempt-but-shown, out of the denominator, gallop checkpoint judging emerges free ¬∑ tremolo SPAN credit (merged `tr@` windows, 100ms buckets, ‚â•60% presence, members light together, ONE unit both sides of the % ‚Äî `_ptScoredUnits`) ¬∑ global `ho`/`po` exemption (judge the picked opener) ¬∑ `ptSpeakBudget(f0)` post-roll physics (clamp(3¬∑period+25, 35, 80)ms, midpoint-clamped) ¬∑ disclosure UX: modal rows (too-fast/slurred/tremolo-units) + **timing-tendency** ("leaned late ~Nms", median dev, gated ‚â•8 & ‚â•30ms) + near-miss aggregate + the resting-strip **pre-run denominator line** (consistency-guarded vs the live classifier) + the **dwell chip** (named exempt class under the playhead, ‚â•0.5s merged runs). ### ‚úÖ Rhythm-ladder genre-spanning expansion ‚Äî DESIGNED + Batch 1 BUILT, uncommitted (2026-06-04)
> **~23-agent group-design session** (learning-design CHAIR + rhythm-meter engine + guitar/bass/drum-pedagogy + **18 genre/subgenre idiom lanes**: metal/punk/surf/blues/jazz/funk/latin/reggae/afrobeat/bluegrass/country/gypsy-jazz/new-orleans/norte√±o/tango/flamenco/disco/prog). > **Architecture (load-bearing, unanimous):** ONE genre-NEUTRAL **~11-rung spine** (A¬∑Grid: Subdivisions/16th-Pocket ¬∑ B¬∑Feel: Swing&Shuffle/Displacement + NEW **Gallop&Snap**/**Accent Displacement** ¬∑ C¬∑Pulse-Frame: NEW **Single-String Pulse**[keystone=1 note,palm-mute,low string]/**Half-Double-Time**[goal-card]/Odd-Meters ¬∑ D¬∑Two-Pulses: Over-the-Barline/Metric-Mod[gated]/Polymeter[gated] ¬∑ Capstone **Trade-Bars/Make-a-Groove**). A genre's device attaches ONLY as a `vary[]` step, an app rung in its OWN Style pack, or goal-card prose ‚Äî **NEVER a new band rung** (the anti-bloat rule, same as the chord ladder).
> **Substrate = a `RHYTHM_CELLS` data table** (`fillNotesFromSeq`'s `steps[]` path already tiles bar-commensurate cells ‚Üí the Latin/dotted/gallop/clave wave is CURATION not code) + an `assertRhythmCellsValid` startup guard (every cell sums to whole bars ‚Äî caught a bad Scotch-snap). **tresillo `[3,3,2]` = the cross-idiom atom** (Latin/NOLA/tango/norte√±o point at one def); clave/habanera/afrobeat-bell/flamenco-comp√°s(`12/8:3+3+2+2+2`)/gallop-family all drop in as data. Honest framing: a single line teaches the TIME of a feel, never the ensemble INTERLOCK ("tap the clave's time").
> **Gated (spec'd, not near-term):** prog's NEW flag ‚Äî a per-bar **changing-meter array** `meterSequence:[...]` (simpler than polymeter + more idiomatic ‚Üí ELEVATE ahead of it) ¬∑ the polymeter cell (Tier-3 decoupled phrase-clock + a load-bearing re-lock visual) ¬∑ metric modulation (block-seam). Bass parity ‚âà zero new build but the right hand diverges on 3 rungs (16th-Pocket‚Üíghost-pocket, Gallop‚Üípick/3-finger, Single-String‚Üíroot-pulse; strip CAGED on bass).
> **‚úÖ BUILT (2026-06-04, uncommitted) ‚Äî Batch 1, verified.** Christian chose "all of Batch 1 in one go." Landed: **`RHYTHM_CELLS` table** (gallop/reverse_gallop moved in + skip_chug/snap + tresillo/son_clave/rumba_clave/habanera, all in BEAT units) + **`assertRhythmCellsValid`** startup guard (sums-to-whole-beats; mirrors no-unison) + `rhythmSteps` reads it ¬∑ **`buildRhythmPulseExercise`** = the new `rhythm_pulse` generator (one palm-muted low-string note, the cell, a movable `pulseAccent` 0‚Äì3) ‚Üí dispatch + `readConfig` `pulseAccent` + screen.html hidden input + practiceType `<option>` + 6 new subdivision `<option>`s ¬∑ **5 new spine rungs** (`rhy_gallop_snap`/`rhy_accent_displace`/`rhy_single_string`/`rhy_half_double`/`rhy_trade_bars`) + the `concept_rhythm` band reordered into the 11-rung 4-strata spine + 5 pathway `<option>`s ¬∑ the **tresillo + son_clave cross-idiom cells wired** (subdivision options + varys on Single-String Pulse = "tap the clave's time on one note"). **Verified:** `node --check`; ### ‚úÖ COMMITTED ‚Äî Chord Concept ladder, Phases A + B (2026-06-04)
> The **`concept_chords`** pack (Concepts family, **guitar-only**), 7 rungs over `strum_comp`, triads/grips SOUNDED TOGETHER (vs the Triads ladder's arpeggios):
> - **Phase A** (`81071d1`, pushed): **Cowboy Chords** ‚Üí **The Five CAGED Shapes** ‚Üí **Barre Chords** ‚Üí **Comping the Changes** (triad/power). Adds `voicingPosition` (open/movable) + `strumPattern` hidden fields, read in `readConfig` + consumed by `buildStrumCompExercise`.
> - **Phase B** (the STRUM_GRIPS unlock): a **separate `STRUM_GRIPS` movable-grip table** (7th/9th/11th/13th/sus ‚Äî do NOT bloat CAGED) consulted in `pickStrumGrip` before the triad fallback, so 7ths voice the 7th instead of reducing to a triad and 9/11/13 voice at all. 3 new rungs: **Sevenths Around the Neck** (min7/maj7/dom7, E+A barre forms over ii‚ÄìV‚ÄìI) ‚Üí **The Harmonized Key** (the diatonic-7th lap `[1..7]`, incl. the dorian IV7 carrier) ‚Üí **Color: 9ths, 11ths & 13ths** (funk dom9, neo-soul min9/min11, big-band dom13, sus ‚Äî dom9 labelled honestly, never "11"). Startup guard `assertStrumGripsValid` machine-proves every grip's pcs ‚äÜ its `CHORD_FORMULAS` stack + no same-MIDI unison + no impossible finger (one finger ‚âÝ two frets). **Reviewed: harmony-theory GO-no-fixes (ratified the fuller dom13, the auto-override modal honesty); guitar-pedagogy GO-with-fixes (3 `fg` finger-hint bugs fixed + the finger-collision guard added).** Verified: `probe-chords-b.mjs` (extensions voice ‚â•4 distinct pcs, not triad reductions) + `probe-chords.mjs` regression + full 13-suite `npm test` EXIT 0.
> **Phase C DEFERRED:** inversions-as-grips + the descending-bass slash token (harmony's rung 6). **Bonus unblocked:** STRUM_GRIPS now supplies the dom9/sus grips the deferred funk-dom9 + pop-sus *palette* wiring were waiting on. Memory `project_chord_concept_ladder`. **Both phases committed to `main`; Phase A pushed, Phase B local ‚Äî push when asked.**

### ‚úÖ Dev-ops e2e screen.js AUDIT + host bigger-picture refresh (2026-06-05, post-release)
> **The audit** (full report in dev-ops agent memory `project_screenjs_e2e_audit`, skill-scoped path): 2 real findings, 1 heads-up, 1 minor; everything else verified clean (error handling, host-API guards, resource hygiene, state machine, storage, injection surface).
> - **‚úÖ FIXED same day ‚Äî the "sideways stop" teardown hole:** regenerate-while-playing / leave-via-nav went through `stopRenderer()` which skipped `sessionEnd()` + `releaseWakeLock()` ‚Üí the screen stayed awake forever AND an abandoned run flushed later with wiped hit/miss counts = a FAKE CLEAN PASS crediting tiers/proof-loop. Fix: `stopRenderer` now closes the session (scorer state still alive) + releases the lock when stopping mid-play. Guard PROMOTED into `smoke-renderers` ("wakelock-pair" row; the probe stays local). Net 15/15.
> - **‚è≠Ô∏è QUEUED (do before pushing long Workouts; pairs with the backing-engine ¬ß14 work): rolling-window audio scheduler.** Play on a 30-min Woodshed schedules EVERYTHING up front ‚Äî measured 39,286 nodes / 1.57s main-thread freeze, repeating at the loop wrap mid-practice. Fix = schedule ~30‚Äì60s ahead from the frame loop (extend `maybeScheduleLoopAhead`).
> - **Noted:** the PT_HIT_FRAMES floor ‚Äî notes <~80‚Äì120ms can't collect 2 frames, so 16ths above ~150‚Äì160 BPM under-score; accepted (false hit > missed hit); cheap follow-up = 1 frame for notes <100ms if dogfooding feels it. Minor: a first-load attach race can orphan a renderer (generation-counter fix, low priority).
> **The host refresh** (slopsmith-host-expert memory `project_host_refresh_2026-06-05`, skill-scoped; host = 0.2.9-beta.1 @ ca3be33): **piano is pre-WIP host-side** (viz-only plugin moved out of core; no track format; no MIDI input) ‚Äî deferral stands, budget an in-tree piano-roll renderer someday. **Backing-engine intel:** `nam_tone` NO LONGER BUNDLED in core ‚Üí vendor-the-worklet vs feature-detect+degrade is a Christian decision at build time (AGPL relicense bears on it; plugins exempt but curated-list needs a compatible license ‚Äî SlopScale ships NO license file); the chord-event timeline = confirmed genuine build (nothing to borrow); `lib/drums.py` GM vocabulary = borrow as the drum-voice naming reference; Minigames SDK now CORE-bundled (grading reaches Desktop users). **WATCH:** the host's capability-runtime pivot (our APIs are tracked compat bridges; the upcoming `note-detection` capability formalizes our #254 gems hook ‚Äî now pinned by a host test), a future viz registry (highway_3d borrow). **DEV-OPS FOLLOW-UPS:** the Desktop install is repackaged (Electron asar) ‚Üí `launch.ps1`'s `bundled` mode is DEAD (fix/retire) + #650 Stage-2 unverifiable from disk + the SessionStart gate hook checks a path that no longer exists (update/retire the hook).

### ‚úÖ Real-audio scoring e2e PROVEN ‚Üí PROMOTED ‚Üí and it caught a REAL grader bug, FIXED (2026-06-05, post-release)
> Christian challenged "have you tested the tuner/grading hooks with Slopsmith?" ‚Äî honest answer was NO (smoke-gems injects a FAKE scorer by design; nobody had played real audio at the real detector). Built the real test: a synthesized 110 Hz A2 WAV streamed via Chromium's fake-mic flags ‚Üí the HOST's real detector ‚Üí the meter reads "A2" ‚Üí grading lights `hit` ‚Üí accuracy counts. ALL PASS ‚Äî note detection genuinely works on current Slopsmith.
> - **PROMOTED per the dev-ops consult ‚Üí `smoke-scoring-e2e.mjs`** (suite #15; a genuinely new SYSTEM ‚Äî the only real-audio test). Consult verdict implemented in full: SDK-absent host = hard-FAIL with a named message (a skip would swallow the #1 thing the suite catches); WAV ‚Üí tmpdir + per-PID + unlink; WEIGHTS entry; added to `test:seq` (run-all glob-discovers, the chain is hand-maintained); console-error capture with NO benign list (scoring failures ARE the point); bundle stashed once; **a negative control** (same tone, drill re-keyed to D ‚Üí no `hit` allowed). Net = **15/15 at 17.4s** (fits in renderers' shadow). Dev-ops memory `project_mic_e2e_promotion`.
> - **‚≠ê The negative control caught a REAL grader bug on its first run:** the detector's lock-on SWEEPS from startup garbage through the ¬±50¬¢ window (measured: +4023¬¢ ‚Üí +485¬¢ ‚Üí ‚àí285¬¢ converging on a ‚àí500¬¢ wrong note) and the single-frame grader permanently scored the false frame ‚Äî every drill's FIRST note could false-hit, inflating the proof-loop's clean-run gate. **FIXED (`ptOnPitch`): `PT_HIT_FRAMES = 2` consecutive in-tune frames (~80ms) required to score**; streak resets on out-of-tune/start/stop. Verified: e2e positive still hits, negative clean, full net green.
> - **Small slice (logged):** the accuracy readout can momentarily show hits > passed ("2/1 (200%)") ‚Äî `_ptScored.size` vs `passedTotal` counting drift in `ptOnPitch`; cosmetic (the suite WARNs, doesn't gate). Related 30-min check: confirm the proof-loop verdict does NOT share this inflatable counter.
> - **Mic-permission affordance DOWNGRADED to small-polish** (was flagged urgent): the e2e proved the pitch meter IS a visible on-state signal and the browser prompts on first play; the only gap is the denied/failed state (meter silently absent, no retry). Zero-code mitigation = a line in the v0.7.3 Discord thread ("no meter = browser blocked the mic").
> - **DECISION (Christian, 2026-06-05): the next BIG slice = the BACKING ENGINE** (docs/backing-engine-roundtable.md) ‚Äî chosen over piano/drums ("Def backing engine"; piano is still WIP host-side anyway). A slopsmith-host-expert bigger-picture refresh (host piano status, borrowable backing capabilities, host direction) ran the same day ‚Äî see its agent memory.

### ‚úÖ DECISION (2026-06-03) ‚Äî STAY A PLUGIN, do NOT register as a Slopsmith minigame
> Christian's reframe (host plain *plugins* look utilitarian; SlopScale's contained player + four-mode shell + gamified progression *feel* more "minigame-like") went to a **5-agent panel** (slopsmith-host-expert ‚Üí gamification + market + learning-design + ux). **Unanimous: stay a plugin.** Verdicts in each agent's `.claude/agent-memory/`.
> **The deciding fact (host-expert, verified vs checkout 0.2.9-alpha.7):** a Slopsmith "minigame" is NOT a higher tier or a separate prestige section ‚Äî it's a `minigame` block + `register()` that drops you into a **host-owned single-round HARNESS** (modifier-picker modal ‚Üí host stage + a host **Quit** button ‚Üí play ONE round ‚Üí the *host's* score/Play-Again results modal; navigate-away = force-teardown). That's a **lower-altitude** container than our four-mode app, and the host runSummary modal would **hijack our proof-loop summary**. Host gamification is shallow (flat global XP + a **local-only** best-score leaderboard + XP-threshold unlocks; **no streaks/achievements/competency model**) ‚Üí **nothing on the progression side to borrow** that would save building our own; our proof-loop + Depth Ladder is strictly richer.
> **Per lane:** gamification ‚Äî host best-score board = exactly the score/rank dark pattern we cut; market ‚Äî a games-hub tile **buckets us with novelty toys** + cheapens the serious-tool identity, and discoverability isn't our binding constraint (self-hosting friction + the proof readout + word-of-mouth are); learning-design ‚Äî a single round can't hold a ladder or a multi-block Workout, and "score" framing nudges mastery‚Üíperformance goals; ux ‚Äî category error, the round stage fights a persistent multi-mode workspace.
> **The "feed host XP/leaderboard WITHOUT registering" hybrid (endpoints ARE callable w/o `register`): DEFERRED** ‚Äî buys ~nothing now (no hub tile without the manifest; XP is a meaningless 2nd currency; a best-score feed fights our competency readout). IF ever taken: feed **competency events (clean-rung verdicts) not rounds/time**, one-way, **invisible in our UI**, decorative-never-load-bearing.
> **Instead (cheap, on-mission):** (1) stay a plugin ‚Äî keep nav screen + four-mode shell + contained playback (zero work); (2) earn "first-class" by craft ‚Äî a sharper **practice/verb-framed nav label + a distinct nav icon** + a strong first-paint mode-overview identity (queued with slopscale-ux-designer); the **proof card** is the outward discoverability hook, not a hub tile; (3) the one good idea the round model surfaced ‚Äî a **capstone "test"/Score-Attack layer** is pedagogically legit, but build it INSIDE our player at the top of a rung's arc crediting a competency (the proof-loop already aspires to this), never via the host harness; (4) north-star guardrail added to CLAUDE/AGENTS: *gamification describes mastery, never substitutes a score for it.*

## üéöÔ∏è Backing-Engine Rebuild ‚Äî DESIGNED 2026-06-03 ¬∑ **plan v2 LOCKED + BUILD STARTED 2026-06-05**

Full charette on the **chord-progression + backing-track + harmony/metric** engines: *make it
better per-genre + more lifelike; what's the USP.* Panel = harmony-theory (chair) + rhythm-meter +
sound-design + audio-engine + drum-pedagogy + market + learning-design + bass/piano-pedagogy + **25
genre lanes** (shoegaze/surf/emo/punk held out as texture/lead-only). **Full spec + per-genre
signature table + decision log: `docs/backing-engine-roundtable.md`; durable synthesis: memory
`project_backing_engine_roundtable`.**

**2026-06-05: an 11-lane panel re-check (the build-owning lanes, background agents) re-validated the
spec against everything shipped since ‚Äî synthesis + locked decisions in the doc's "Build-plan v2"
addendum** (per-lane detail in each agent's `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/project_backing_*`).
Plan-changers: the timeline keystone is **~40% already shipped** (`compileChordTimeline` exists,
backing + proof metric read it ‚Äî step 1 shrinks to finishing it + two per-block assembly fixes);
**one cell grammar** (COMP_GROOVES = the STRUM_PATTERNS grid with object steps; RHYTHM_CELLS = the
shared timing atoms via a `cellOnsets` bridge); the **rolling-window scheduler is step 0**
(unanimous); articulation costs **zero extra nodes** (automation on the WAF-returned GainNode);
mix 7a (velocity tiers + ARTIC envelopes) ships **inside** step 3; backing bass lands **ROOT on 1**
kick-locked (flip of Connect's guide-tone preference); drums rename to the host `lib/drums.py`
vocab; seeded determinism baked at generation (byte-golden charts). **Christian's locked decisions:**
(1) **build all ~9 taught genres BEFORE release** (overrides the panel's ship-one-and-measure rec);
jazz = the vertical pilot through steps 3‚Äì5, blues = the A/B control; (2) **NAM = in-house
WaveShaper + CC0 cab-IR chain + feature-detect `nam_tone`** (NO vendoring ‚Äî upstream is unlicensed;
follow-ups: clear a CC0 IR + add our repo LICENSE); (3) **proof-loop flag ON with this build**;
(4) minors per panel rec: REF_TRIM fader-unity defaults, funk goes Dorian, pushed landings credit
the seam proof, `backingDensity` authored-only, A/B pad-vs-comp toggle = dev flag.

**Diagnosis:** the harmony is right (`COMMON_PROGRESSIONS` + the `voiceChord` engine are good); the
whole **rhythm/texture layer is missing**. Backing = exactly TWO comp shapes ‚Äî one sustained voiced
**pad/bar** + the **blues boogie** ‚Äî harmony **bar-locked**, backing **bass = the pad's sustained
root**, **4 drum grooves**, **one global swing**. So every non-blues genre plays *a held chord over a
rock backbeat*. Fix = recombinable **PRIMITIVES**, NOT 30 canned palettes (north star).

**USP (market):** the backing is a **teaching instrument wired to the drill + the fretboard mirror**,
not an accompaniment ‚Äî the only loop nobody else closes (iReal accompanies/never teaches; BiaB
lifelike/inert; Chordify song-locked). **Only true differentiator = voice-leading + harmonic rhythm
tied to the Jam mirror.** Per-genre feel for already-taught genres = **table-stakes**; **30+ palettes
= sprawl/DRIFT** (this is the **#1 off-mission magnet**). **Drift bright line:** *better-PLAYING vs
better-SOUNDING-unattended* ‚Üí loop a vamp NOT arrange a song; no arrangement sections; **no backing
export**; no "make me a jam" entry without a drill; Jam stays a mirror.

**KEYSTONE (unanimous) = the beat-based CHORD-EVENT TIMELINE** (chords on beats, `durBeats`,
`push`/anticipation, engine-*generated* passing/approach chords) ‚Äî this **IS** the deferred
**Playing-changes Stage 2** (`compileChordTimeline`); bar-lock becomes the trivial case. Everything
rides it.

**Primitive registries:** `COMP_GROOVES` (per-hit target/artic incl. **mute-chug/arpeggiate/swell/
pump/roll/arrastre**, **per-beat `slots`** = the country keystone, `arpPattern` note-order,
`cellBars`/`cellBeats`, **`compLanes[]` ‚â•2 concurrent lanes**, `couple/unison`) ¬∑ `BASS_FIGURES`
(incl. **generated** `motown_counter`/`walking` reusing Connect, the **`tresillo` 3-3-2 atom**,
`808_glide`, `connectBass` walk-up) ¬∑ genre `DRUM_GROOVES` (+ride/rim/openHat/bell lanes, **fills**,
seeded kit-gated humanization, `drums:none`/percussion-role comp) ¬∑ **voice-leading between backing
chords** + `voicingStyle` {tertian|quartal|shell|drop2|rootless|drone} + `chromatic_mediant` ¬∑
per-lane/per-recipe **swing + swing-LOCK + per-voice split** + half/double-time + swung-16ths +
triplet-subdiv. **Lifelike = GESTURE not timbre** ‚Äî a per-hit **envelope layer on the existing WAF
sampler** (ZERO new assets) + **kill the sustained pad** (sound-design's #1 fix). `STYLE_PALETTES`
become thin **recipes** over the registries (adding a genre = pick ~5 primitives, zero new code;
startup guard mirrors no-unison).

**Build order v2 (2026-06-05 ‚Äî supersedes the original ¬ß7 order; full detail in the doc's
"Build-plan v2" addendum):** **0** rolling-window scheduler (¬ß14 ‚Äî ‚â§50ms play-press, ‚â§2k live
nodes typical; `_ptStreak` wrap-reset rides along) ‚Üí **1** finish `chart.timeline` (sub-bar
`durBeats`, `push` clamped at count-in/loop seam, `bass` override, approach tags; keyCycle +
per-block session assembly fixes; determinism assert + the new `smoke-backing-engine.mjs` land
here) ‚Üí **2** voice-leading between backing chords (thread `prevVoicing`, piano's comper rule-set,
in-voicer hand-span/low-interval guards; modal-M1 tokens + funk-Dorian ride along) ‚Üí **3**
`COMP_GROOVES` (unified grammar) + pad-kill + mix-7a + `backingDensity` + player-is-the-comp
suppression; boogie migrates to a recipe as the proof ‚Üí **3.5** mix-7b (shared reverb/pan/carve ‚Äî
before drums) ‚Üí **4** `BASS_FIGURES` (root-on-1 kick-locked; boogie = figure #1; walking + motown
generators) ‚Üí **5** genre `DRUM_GROOVES` + fills same batch (lib/drums.py rename first; seeded
humanize) ‚Üí **6** palette-as-recipe refactor + guard, then the remaining 8 genres' recipes (each
vetted by its genre-idiom agent) before release ‚Üí **DEFER behind proof:** `compLanes[]` multi-lane
(reggae bubble, afrobeat interlock, bluegrass roll), multi-bar/polymeter cells (`cellBeats` ‚Äî Latin
clave, flamenco comp√°s, prog unison), swung-16ths (`swingUnit`), the exotic articulations +
passing-chord generator + quartal/drop2 + `busy_melodic`.

**Discipline (market + L&D): right thing, RIGHT order.** NOW = unbreak the ~9 taught genres +
voice-leading (the proof-loop payload). DEFER = palette breadth + the exotic-meter lanes. **Proof
metric** = seam guide-tone-landing + drill‚ÜíJam return-rate (already instrumented via Connect), NOT
minutes-jammed ‚Äî and it **gates** the breadth tier. **L&D payoff order:** harmonic-rhythm >
voice-leading > comp-grooves > basslines > drums > breadth. Dovetails with **Modal M7/M9** (give
`modal_vamp` a comp/backing layer; sparse modal comp + slow harmonic rhythm) and **Drums Phase D5/D6**
(humanization + genre grooves) below ‚Äî same registries.

## üéº Modal Harmony & Modal Progressions ‚Äî full-panel audit + To-Do (2026-06-02)

15-agent panel (harmony-theory **CHAIR** + learning-design + guitar/bass/piano-pedagogy + 10 broad genre-idiom agents ‚Äî jazz/rock/funk/prog/blues/country/classical/metal/pop/latin; subgenre agents excluded per Christian). Q: are we accounting for modal harmony/progressions in everything built so far? **Verdict: PARTIAL** ‚Äî modal SCALES ‚úÖ complete; harmony ENGINE ‚úÖ already modally correct (`DIATONIC_QUALITIES` has per-mode quality rows; modal vamps produce characteristic chords; **no functional-V7 smuggling** ‚Äî a modal vamp has no degree-5 to functionalize); but modal HARMONY-as-content is half-built and modal VOCABULARY is barely taught. Full per-lane specs in `.claude/agent-memory/<agent>/`; durable synthesis in memory `project_modal_harmony_audit`. (`COMMON_PROGRESSIONS` has ~28 keys, not 17 ‚Äî `static_i`/`minor_ii_V_i`/`rhythm_changes_a`/`quick_change_blues` live there; no second table.)

**The gaps (cross-panel consensus):**
- Only the **dark/minor** modal family ships (Aeolian `i-‚ô≠VII-‚ô≠VI`, Phrygian-metal); the **bright** family (Mixolydian `I-‚ô≠VII-IV`, Dorian `i-IV`/`i7-IV7`, Lydian `I-II`, So-What/sus, clean Phrygian `I-‚ô≠II`) is documented in `docs/theory-progressions.md` but **NOT in `COMMON_PROGRESSIONS`** ‚Üí `STYLE_PALETTES`/Jam/Custom/Workouts **can't play a Mixolydian groove or a Dorian vamp**.
- Modes taught as neutral **scale shapes**, not **vocabulary** ‚Äî the characteristic note (Dorian ‚ôÆ6 / Mixo ‚ô≠7 / Lydian ‚ôØ4 / Phrygian ‚ô≠2) is never emphasized/felt.
- Curriculum arc **upside-down** ‚Äî the *easy* static-modal ear skill is buried in Advanced `modal_vamp`; the *hard* mode-of-moment "play the changes" is what "modal" means everywhere else.
- **Bass** groove grip modally **inert** (`bassRootGrip` = root/5th/octave, never reads `cfg.scale`) ‚Üí `scale:'dorian'` on a bass groove is decorative.
- **No quartal/So-What voicing**; no `nonFunctional`/`modalColor` voicing intent (bury the tritone ‚Äî the inverse of the changes-voicer).
- **prog/classical/latin have no `STYLE_PALETTES` entry** (no Jam; classical palette-less by design).
- `modal_vamp` routes to `buildScaleExercise` (bare run + drone, **no comp/backing layer**).

**Per-genre #1 modal gap:** jazz=Dorian So-What/Impressions m7 vamp + sus-vamp ¬∑ rock=Mixolydian `I-‚ô≠VII-IV` ¬∑ funk=Dorian `i7-`**`IV7`** (IV7 carries the ‚ôÆ6; `static_i` is a bare drone) ¬∑ blues=static dom7 "Mixolydian-is-home" vamp + minor-blues Dorian (‚ô≠7-as-home) ¬∑ country=Mixolydian ‚ô≠VII "train chord" (else country == pop) ¬∑ pop=Aeolian `i-‚ô≠VI-‚ô≠III-‚ô≠VII` dark loop ¬∑ prog=no palette + Lydian `I-II` + modal interchange ¬∑ classical=Phrygian cadence + leading-tone-free modal cadences (church-modes √©tude/counterpoint) ¬∑ latin=no palette + Dorian montuno (clave-gated) ¬∑ **metal=STRONGEST, taught as vocabulary** ‚Äî only add `phrygian_dominant` as a LEAD scale.

**Token trap (rock/country/funk/pop all independently flagged):** the ‚ô≠VII/‚ô≠II/major-IV must be `{semis:‚Ä¶}` tokens with explicit major/dom7 qualities ‚Äî a bare degree-7 silently sounds Aeolian. Ship modal vamps `chordOverride:'auto'`, **never `'dom7'`** (only `andalusian` needs `{5:'dom7'}`).

**Phased To-Do (M1‚ÄìM16):**
- **Phase 0 ‚Äî engine foundation (KEYSTONE):** **M1 ‚úÖ BUILT (2026-06-02)** ‚Äî 8 bright-modal progression tokens (`mixolydian_rock`/`mixolydian_vamp`/`dorian_vamp`/`lydian_vamp`/`so_what`/`phrygian_vamp`/`andalusian`/`modal_mixture`) + `PROGRESSION_QUALITY_OVERRIDES.andalusian={5:'dom7'}` in `COMMON_PROGRESSIONS`; bare degrees so the paired mode supplies the quality (Phrygian ‚ô≠II pinned `q:'maj'`). Verified by `probe-modal.mjs` (8/8 modal chords correct ‚Äî anti-trap cases pass: Mixo ‚ô≠VII=maj7, Dorian IV=dom7, Phrygian ‚ô≠II=maj) + full 9-suite smoke; harmony-theory-architect sign-off GO. **Dormant until M4 wires them** (no palette/dropdown ref yet). ¬∑ **M2** quartal/So-What voicing primitive (So-What = 3 stacked 4ths + a maj-3rd on top) ¬∑ **M3** `nonFunctional`/`modalColor` voicing intent (suppress the tritone, omit the leading tone).
- **Phase 1 ‚Äî wire styles:** **M4** per-genre palette wiring ¬∑ **M5** add `prog` + `latin` palettes (latin gated on a clave-locked rhythm cell ‚Äî don't ship "modal chords + a straight click").
- **Phase 2 ‚Äî feel the mode:** **M6** characteristic-note emphasis pass (within the shape's fret window, no added shift) ¬∑ **M7** give `modal_vamp` a comp/backing layer ¬∑ **M8** modal-aware bass grip + Dorian/Mixo/Phrygian static-vamp bass templates (kill the decorative-`scale` trap) ¬∑ **M9** sparse-sustained modal comp + slow harmonic rhythm (chord change every 4‚Äì8 bars).
- **Phase 3 ‚Äî curriculum:** **M10** static-modal as an ear skill in late Beginner ‚Üí harmonic concept in Intermediate ‚Üí Advanced `modal_vamp` reframed to exotic scales ¬∑ **M11** distinguish static-modal vs play-the-changes; add a Modal-vamp *flavor* to the existing Application Workout role ¬∑ **M12** verdict-signal engine gap (a characteristic-tone / non-resolution success signal, else modal grades like functional).
- **Phase 4 ‚Äî content:** **M13** goal-cards NAME the device (jazz "play over a center"; blues "‚ô≠7 is home"; country "the ‚ô≠VII train chord") ¬∑ **M14** new/expanded pathways per genre (modal-jazz, Mixolydian rock, Dorian funk, dom7/minor blues, country ‚ô≠VII, prog interchange, classical church-modes + Phrygian cadence, latin montuno, dark-pop Aeolian) ‚Äî each vetted by its idiom + pedagogy agent.
- **Phase 5 ‚Äî deferred/gated:** **M15** piano modal design (quartal/So-What + `modalColor`) ‚Äî gated on the piano `hand`/`finger`/`positionContext` schema ¬∑ **M16** two unbuilt primitives surfaced ‚Äî modal two-voice counterpoint (classical; `harmonize:true` only does parallel dyads) + the clave-locked rhythm cell (latin).

**Build order:** M1 is the keystone ‚Äî ship the progression tokens first (harmony's note-spelling sign-off gates everything). Then palettes (M4) for immediate Jam payoff ‚Üí feel (M6‚ÄìM8) ‚Üí curriculum + content. On-mission throughout (it *names the grammar* ‚Äî gallop, So-What, the ‚ô≠VII train chord ‚Äî not "generate a song"; metal is the proof that modal-as-vocabulary lands). **NEXT (M1 done):** M4 ‚Äî wire the new tokens into `STYLE_PALETTES` (immediate Jam/Custom payoff) + the Custom progression dropdown, per the per-genre #1 map above; then M2 (quartal voicing) + M6‚ÄìM8 (feel). When `andalusian` later gets a harmonic-minor/phrygian-dominant pairing, add it to `MINOR_SPELLED_PROGRESSIONS` (harmony's M4 forward-note).

## üîß Workout backing/notes/click desync ‚Äî FIXED (2026-06-02)

User-reported: in multi-block Workouts the backing track drifted off the visual notes + click. **Root cause:** `makeBundle` synthesized ALL backing from ONE cfg (the session's first-block metadata) over the whole duration, while `buildSessionChart` assembles notes+beats **per-block** (own tempo/meter/key + inter-block breaks). Diagnosed with a probe (10 backing events inside a break gap; single-config Pathways/Custom/Jam were clean). 3-agent fix consult (rhythm-meter chair + harmony + sound-design). Memory: `project_workout_backing_desync_fix`.
- **FIX:** backing is now assembled **per-block** in `buildSessionChart` (each block's comp/bass/drums on its own `segCfg`, swung on its own grid in block-local time, offset onto the timeline; the break gap is backing-silent for free). `makeBundle` branches on `chart.backingEvents` ‚Äî sessions use the pre-assembled per-block backing + skip the global swing; single exercises unchanged. Extracted `swungTime`/`swingNotesBacking` so swing is per-block (the global `applySwingToBundle` warped later blocks against block-1's grid).
- **Follow-on 2 (per-rung):** the rung builders (`buildBpmLadderChart`/`buildKeyCycleChart`) now emit their OWN per-rung backing (built+swung at each rung's tempo/key); `fillBlockToDuration` tiles it; consumers prefer `chart.backingEvents`. Fixes ladder (per-rung tempo) + key-cycle (per-rung key) backing ‚Äî incl. the **pre-existing single-exercise** key-cycle/ladder case.
- **Guard:** `smoke-session-sync.mjs` (`npm run smoke:sync`; `npm test` is now **10 suites**) ‚Äî backing tracks per-block/rung tempo+key, silent in the break, single-config unaffected. Harmony bonus: a Dorian/`static_i` block now voices its OWN scale (was inheriting block-1's mode ‚Üí the M1 modal vamps in a Workout now sound right).
- **RULE (rhythm-meter):** *every timed array must be assembled in the same per-block loop, or it desyncs.* `backingEvents` + swing were the two that had escaped it.
- **Follow-on 1 (DONE ‚Äî `b4c669a`, shipped in v0.7.1):** a band re-entry fade. harmony+bass+drums now route through a dedicated **backing-group** gain node (click/notes bypass it; Mixer faders stay upstream); `scheduleBackingEnvelope` rides it for a ~18 ms fade-out into each break + a ~18 ms fade-in on the next downbeat (breaks = gaps in `segmentBounds`, scheduled at absolute ctx-time per pass). Single-exercise modes = no-op at unity. The audible result is a play-test item; smoke confirms no throw.

## üß™ Golden-file regression for the generator core ‚Äî DESIGNED, DEFERRED (2026-06-02)

4-agent review (harmony-theory + slopsmith-host-expert + rhythm-meter + market-analyst) of Christian's idea: commit reference generator outputs as golden files; a `test` command diffs new output ‚Üí intentional-vs-regression, protecting the core's stability while the standalone-fork path stays open. **Verdict: SOUND idea, the panel refined it into a genuinely good design ‚Äî but DEFER behind the proof-loop + the in-flight modal/transport work.** Full synthesis + the build spec in memory `project_golden_file_harness`.

- **Premise fix (unanimous):** the core is **JavaScript** (`generateExercise`/`generateSession` ‚Üí `{version,session,chart}`), NOT "pure-Python" ‚Äî `routes.py` is the dormant shell. Golden the JS **chart**.
- **The refined design (build THIS when triggered):**
  - **Boundary that kills the re-bless treadmill:** byte-golden the core **chart** (pre-`makeBundle`); **property-**assert the bundle's feel layer (count-in / swing / `_tail`) ‚Äî those live downstream of the core, so they fall outside the chart golden automatically.
  - **Snapshot the pitch-CLASS SET, not the MIDI voicing** ‚Äî locks *what the chord is* (IP) while leaving *where it sits on the neck* (by-ear register) free ‚Üí near-zero churn on tuning.
  - **Reference set = the RISK surface** (not "C-scale + arp + lick", which just re-tests plumbing the smokes cover): voiceChord maj/min parity, qualities across modes, the **M1 Mixo/Dorian vamp**, a tritone-sub, a **Connect ii‚ÄìV‚ÄìI lick**, + a **7/8 (2+2+3) drill** (the keystone time case) + property-asserted count-in / swung / BPM-ladder bundle cases. Share fixtures across pitch+time.
  - **Build, two tiers:** Tier-1 = clone the Playwright/`smoke-core-purity` pattern (ships today but *rides the host ‚Üí doesn't advance decoupling*). **Tier-2 (the prize)** = ~30-line plain-Node, gated behind a ~5-line seam (guard the IIFE bootstrap's `document` touches + a `globalThis` export ‚Äî the half-built `__SS_HARNESS__` hook). Goldens live **core-adjacent** (travel with the core into a standalone repo), `--update` flag = an intentional change is a reviewed git diff. Determinism: seed/avoid `Math.random` on the ref path; keep `.toFixed(6)` rounded values.
  - **Complements (‚âÝ overlaps) `smoke-core-purity.mjs`:** purity guards COUPLING ("can it be lifted out"); goldens guard OUTPUT STABILITY ("does the lifted-out core still behave"). Highest value = the safety net **for the extraction diff itself**.
- **Market's dissent (why deferred):** premature infra that presupposes the extraction it protects; no 2nd consumer yet (CLAUDE.md: no standalone scaffolding until one exists); existing smoke + integrity guards already catch player-relevant regressions; re-bless tax bites hardest during the current modal/transport churn; the build slot belongs to the proof-loop (Phase-9 readouts + ~5 players).
- **TRIGGER to build:** when the engine has **stabilized** (modal arc + transport settled) **OR extraction begins** ‚Äî whichever first; the Tier-2 de-DOM seam is the natural first step of extraction. Optional opportunistic now: the Tier-2 seam alone (~5 lines, reversible, independently useful).

- **The 9-phase plan** (tasks #1‚Äì#9; deps 5‚Üê{1,2,3} ¬∑ 6‚Üê{1,4} ¬∑ 7‚Üê{5,6} ¬∑ 8‚Üê1 ¬∑ 9‚Üê1): 1 ‚úÖ ¬∑ 2 ‚úÖ ¬∑ 3 ‚úÖ(partial‚ÜíP5) ¬∑ 4 ‚úÖ ¬∑ 5 ~40 guitar templates **(+ the carried funk/pop STRUM_GRIPS wiring)** ¬∑ 6 ~25 bass templates ¬∑ 7 ~20 starter sessions (role-skeletons) ¬∑ 8 `slopscale.progress` + refresh‚ÜíTravel ¬∑ 9 UX (library drawer + editable timeline + refresh + starter grid).

## üèãÔ∏è Workout-pillar + curriculum-scaling charette (2026-06-02) ‚Äî APPROVED (spine + keep-27); validating Core-Beginner next, then build

A launch-scope 5-agent group-design charette (chaired by `learning-design-architect`, 2 waves: + `market-analyst`, then `gamification-architect` + `slopscale-ux-designer` + `harmony-theory-architect`; main thread synthesized). Question: make Custom + Workout top-tier, design a "Workout building-block framework" wide for launch, an auto-planner/"coach" for the player who doesn't know what to practice, genre incorporation, more pathways + more exercises-per-pathway. **Full per-lane specs in `.claude/agent-memory/`** (`learning-design-architect/project_workout_framework_and_planner`, `market-analyst/library-size-and-planner`, + the gamification/ux/harmony files).

**Core finding ‚Äî primitive-RICH, content-THIN.** We have ~29 exercise primitive types, ~28 scales, ~30 progressions, but only **4 Workout templates** and **27 THIN pathways (~2‚Äì4 rungs vs a credible 6‚Äì10)**. So "go wide" = **composition + depth, NOT new generators** ‚Äî with ONE justified exception (`strum_comp`, below). **The Workout pillar is the single highest-leverage launch investment** (and `targetSec`/`fillBlockToDuration` already exist).

**Library-size benchmark** (field-inferred from comparable practice apps + music-software preset libraries ‚Äî MED confidence, no telemetry yet): credible-at-launch = **12‚Äì20 well-differentiated pathways** (we have 27 ‚Üí count met, **depth missed**), **5‚Äì10 rungs per pathway** (we're at ~2‚Äì4 ‚Üí the real gap), **8‚Äì12 starter Workouts** (we have 4 ‚Üí a stub; target **~10**). Lesson from VST preset-counts: don't chase the integer; make content **browsable/categorized + "full not empty" on first screen**.

**The plan, small ‚Üí big:**
1. *(small)* **Finish the Custom tidy** ‚Äî cut Regenerate; **Copy link prominent, Paste demoted to a quiet text-affordance** (kept, not deleted ‚Äî Custom is where you *load* a shared routine). Answers "is copy/paste too much choice?": trim + de-emphasize, don't remove.
2. *(small)* **Seed the Workout arc** in the UI ‚Äî warm-up ‚Üí technique ‚Üí application as a soft default (path of least resistance, never a lock).
3. *(med)* **Workout block-type framework:** block = `{ role, practiceType (1 of the existing 29), style?, duration }`. Roles = Warm-up / Technique-isolation / Scale-Arp focus / Application-over-changes / Jam / Review / Cool-down. Composition rules (warm-up first; ‚â•1 isolation before application; ‚â§2 same-primitive in a row; Review resurfaces an earlier skill; ~3‚Äì5 blocks / 8‚Äì12 min). **Zero new generators** ‚Äî role is metadata over what exists.
4. *(med)* **Workout authoring flow** ‚Äî the session-progress segment bar becomes an editable timeline; the Inspector becomes the block editor (reuse Custom's practiceType picker + style chips + Feel). "‚âà N min" = a sum readout, not a goal. No second player.
5. *(med)* **~10 vendor starter Workouts** (goal √ó level √ó time) + chip-filtered browse grid (full-not-empty) ‚Äî the authoring quality-bar AND the planner's payload.
6. *(med)* **Shareable Workout** ‚Äî extend the existing `#s=<base64>` link encoder to the whole block array (no accounts/social).
7. *(med)* **Session-end readout** ‚Äî per-block rung-clears roll up into ONE gained-only summary ("a mix bouncing down"), reusing the locked `--ss-meter`/verdict grammar + the in-tempo break-verdict beat. No score/rank.
8. *(big)* **Build `strum_comp` ‚Äî the ONE justified new generator.** Real hole: all 29 primitives are single-note/arpeggiated; nothing strums a **held, voiced chord with a rhythm** ‚Äî the literal skill a beginner rhythm pathway teaches. Serves 3 of the 6 new pathways (Rhythm-Feel, Pop comping, Funk vamp). **Already a locked Guitar-Core decision** ("build comping generator") ‚Äî corroborates, doesn't expand, scope. Pre-build review: rhythm-meter + voicing + guitar-pedagogy.
9. *(big)* **Deepen Core pathways to 6‚Äì10 rungs** (Core-Beginner first). Explicit harmony ladder: pentatonic box ‚Üí +blue note ‚Üí position travel ‚Üí major-pent flip ‚Üí triads ‚Üí 7th vocab ‚Üí guide tones ‚Üí Connect over ii‚ÄìV‚ÄìI (Jam cap). Needs the two Depth-Ladder engine gaps `gamification-architect` owns: **Jam-as-graded "Apply" summit** (post-Jam, opt-in landing-read ‚Äî never grade mid-flow) + **Review = re-bank at the highest cleared rung**.
10. *(big)* **New pathways to fill holes**, prioritized: Rhythm/Strumming-Feel (biggest hole, needs #8) ‚Üí Rock ‚Üí Funk-R&B 16th ‚Üí **Jazz Vocabulary** (ii‚ÄìV‚ÄìI is Workout-only today ‚Äî no jazz *pathway*) ‚Üí Pop comping ‚Üí bass-parity Cores. Each vetted by its genre-idiom + pedagogy agent before "done." Palette wiring gaps to fix: funk `dom9`/`dom13` + a 2-chord vamp; pop doo-wop + sus; jazz `minor_ii_V_i` (qualities all already exist ‚Äî wiring only).
11. *(big, LAST)* **"Suggested today" planner = a light ROUTER, not an AI coach.** One editable, ignorable invite card: *resume your pathway at the next uncleared rung* / *run this N-min set* / ignore. Surfaces **competency** ("next rung"), **never a quota** ("hit 15 min"); **NO streaks / calendars / nags** (gamification: competence-anticipation builds the habit; loss-aversion is the dark pattern we refuse). Genre rides it ‚Äî a "Metal day" just themes the blocks via STYLE_PALETTES.

**DECISIONS ‚Äî APPROVED 2026-06-02 (Christian):** (A) **Spine approved** ‚Äî block = role over the existing 29 primitives, **no new generators except `strum_comp`**; **deepen Core-Beginner before adding new pathways**. (B) **KEEP all 27 pathways and deepen** them (no prune). **NEXT:** guitar/bass-pedagogy + genre-idiom agents validate the Core-Beginner 8-rung ladder + new-pathway content **before build**; the Workout pillar (#1‚Äì#7 ‚Äî finish Custom tidy, framework, authoring, ~10 starter Workouts, share, readout) needs no pedagogy validation and can start in parallel. `strum_comp` (#8) gets rhythm-meter + voicing + guitar-pedagogy review before it's built.

## üé∏ Cross-instrument Workout structure ‚Äî LOCKED (2026-06-02); the spec for building bass next

3-agent design consult (`learning-design-architect` chair + `bass-pedagogy-expert` + `piano-pedagogy-expert`; main thread synthesized). Question: how do Workouts + the practice-type registry span guitar / bass / piano ‚Äî bundle together or fork per instrument? **Answer: neither ‚Äî a 3-layer model.** Per-lane detail in the three agents' `.claude/agent-memory/`; durable synthesis in project memory `project_cross_instrument_workout_structure`.

- **Layer 1 ‚Äî ONE universal framework for every instrument.** The block-type ROLES (Warm-up ‚Üí Technique-isolation ‚Üí Application-over-changes ‚Üí Jam ‚Üí Review) + the arc + the session/`targetSec` structure are shared. Do NOT fork the structure per instrument.
- **Layer 2 ‚Äî ONE shared primitive registry; each practice type carries a TERNARY per-instrument applicability tag:** `native` (as-is) / `adapted` (same primitive, instrument-specific config/feel) / `n-a` (not offered). The **`adapted` middle state is load-bearing** (bass legato = hammer/pull only; bass vibrato slower/narrower; bass "sweep" = a raked broken arp, not a metal sweep) ‚Äî a binary tag would render these guitar-shaped and feel wrong. Formalize via one `offerable(primitive, instrument)` predicate + a startup integrity guard, **replacing** the ad-hoc runtime throws (`bending` throws on bass) + the just-added onLaunchSession same-instrument-family guard.
- **Layer 3 ‚Äî per-instrument CONTENT** composed from the tagged registry.
- **Parity principle:** parallel journeys at the role/competency layer, never forced same at the content layer (same arc + competency themes per tier, bespoke fillings; anti-sameness AND anti-gap guards).

**Bass ‚Äî ~90% right for pitch, optimistic for feel; NO schema change needed.** Of the 29 primitives: ~21 `native`, ~5 `adapted` (legato, vibrato, tapping, pentatonic_super, sweep), ~3 guitar-only (bending, tremolo_picking, hybrid_picking). `position` (movable all-4ths box) is correct, not CAGED/3NPS. **Bass's identity = right hand + groove, and the 29 have almost none of it** ‚Üí add 5 NEW primitives (not recomposable): `root_fifth_octave` (the foundational bass box, taught BEFORE scales ‚Äî highest priority), `slap_pop`, `dead_note_groove` (pocket), `right_hand_technique` (alternating i-m / raking), `octave_groove`. Credible library ‚âà 6‚Äì8 workouts (Bass Foundations shipped ¬∑ Right-Hand Engine ¬∑ Groove & Pocket ¬∑ Walking Bass ¬∑ Slap & Pop ¬∑ Arpeggios & Changes‚Ä¶). **Sequencing nuance:** right-hand + root-fifth-octave + groove come BEFORE scale velocity ‚Äî the opposite emphasis order from a guitar shred ladder (parity of arc, not of order).

**Piano ‚Äî "shared spine + its own technique layer," SCHEMA-GATED.** All theory primitives transfer (scales, arps, guide_tones, chord_scales, bebop, inversions, shell_voicings, walking_bass) ‚Äî piano is their native home ‚Äî via `hand`/`finger`/`positionContext` (thumb-under = the finger sequence). `n-a`: CAGED/3NPS, string_skipping, sweep, bending, hybrid/tremolo picking, pedal_riff, slides/HOPO. Piano's own MUST-HAVE primitives (4): thumb-under scale, thumb-under arpeggio, two-hand coordination, rootless comping + a hand-span guardrail in schema validation (Hanon/position-shifts/pedaling/10ths later). **HARD DEPENDENCY: piano blocks on the planned `hand`/`finger`/`positionContext` schema (Phase 6 groundwork) landing first** ‚Äî design-locked, build-gated.

**Build order:** (1) Guitar ‚Äî done (29 primitives + 11 workouts). (2) **Bass NEXT** ‚Äî no schema change: formalize ternary tags + `offerable()`, add the 5 right-hand/groove primitives, ship ~6‚Äì8 bass workouts in the right sequence (validate new primitives with bass-pedagogy + idiom agents). (3) Piano ‚Äî land the schema + span guard FIRST, then its 4 native primitives + 2 starter workouts.

## üéöÔ∏è Depth Ladder & run-length ‚Äî SPEC LOCKED (2026-06-01), foundation building
Two converged group-design rounds (gamification chaired retention, L&D chaired length; + market + guitar-pedagogy; main thread synthesized). Christian: "lock it in." **Full spec + numbers + the staged build queue live in project memory `project_depth_ladder_and_run_length`** (the canonical record); per-lane detail in the four agents' `.claude/agent-memory/`. Headlines:
- **Replay/level = the Depth Ladder, NOT rep-counting** (rep-gates cut, unanimous). Generalize the shipped tempo "Climb" into a 4-axis finite per-exercise ladder ‚Äî **Speed ‚Üí Travel (key/position) ‚Üí Support-off (metronome/eyes off) ‚Üí Apply (Jam)** ‚Äî each rung gated on a **clean-and-in-time RUN, never reps/raw-BPM** (the load-bearing rule: a rep/BPM gate trains speeding past cleanliness). XP stays **derived (time√ódifficulty), gained-only, never gates**; a maxed exercise keeps earning for *playing*. Mainline-Slopsmith XP = architect the **outbound `slopscale:progress` seam now, defer the live hook**.
- **Run length is content-derived, never a flat clock, and ends with a verdict.** Pass-bounded drills (scale/chromatic/technique) ~30‚Äì50s, hard ceiling ~90s; cycle-bounded drills (chord-scales-over-changes, guide-tones, prog/diatonic arps, full-neck) **legitimately >60s** (unit = the harmonic cycle, ‚â§~3min). Settling-tax verdict window (first 1‚Äì2 passes don't count) kills the 22s-fluke clear. Two currencies: XP scales WITH length, rung-clears LENGTH-NEUTRAL (one clean run clears, any length). Long runs get a silent within-run `--ss-meter` progress lane.
- **Pathway = 6‚Äì10 rungs; "complete" = all rungs cleared ‚Äî measured in rungs, NEVER a wall-clock/minutes readout.** Session dose 10‚Äì20 min across 2‚Äì3 pathways. **No user-facing minutes slider** (expose practice *depth*, not a clock). Jam stays endless; Workout's per-block `targetSec` unchanged ‚Äî this only changes Pathways/Custom drills.
- **Anti-metric (when telemetry exists ‚Äî none yet):** time-per-clear rising while clear-rate-at-spec flat = padding/dark pattern.

**Staged build (length substrate first):** (1) **right-sized finite runs** ‚Äî per-type `RUN_TARGET_SEC` + tier/ladder modifiers + clamps + cycle-completion override ‚Üí the shipped `fillBlockToDuration`; finite-run-ends-with-closure (existing session card) + a "keep looping" toggle ‚Üê **BUILT (commit `33cc69f`, pushed); run-length numbers are FIRST-PASS ‚Äî feel them in practice before slice 2 gates clears on them.** **NEXT ‚Üí (2)** `slopscale.progress` store + clean-and-in-time gate on the Speed Climb (graceful fallback when scoring absent). (3) Depth axes (Travel/Support-off/Apply) + per-axis length modifiers. (4) XP readout + the host emit seam + Off/Casual/Hardcore wiring.

**Also shipped + pushed this session (`origin/main`, through `6396626`):** the Pathways back-half **GUI reorg** (climb-led layout, Notes/Backing/Click practice pills, Mixer TONE knob), the **live fretboard strip on Tab + 3D Highway**, the **1-bar first-run count-in**, and the **core/shell host-independence boundary + `smoke-core-purity` guard** (`npm test` now 7 suites; see memory `project_host_independent_core`).

### ‚è∏Ô∏è STOPPED HERE (2026-06-01) ‚Äî v0.6.0 SHIPPED (pushed + tagged + GitHub release): "Play the Changes" dial + extended-range fix; remaining Stage 2 = the chord-event TIMELINE (+ region, Jam preview)
